She was charged with second-degree murder as a hate crime[[625]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-626) and was sentenced to 24 years imprisonment in 2015.[[626]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-627)

The [American Civil Liberties Union](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Civil_Liberties_Union "American Civil Liberties Union") (ACLU) keeps track of Nationwide Anti-Mosque Activity where they have noted at least 50 anti-mosque incidents in the previous five years.[[627]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-628)

In 2017, a Tennessee man harassed two Muslim girls after they got off a school bus. He yelled at the girls "Go back to your country!". The man injured the father of the girls by assaulting him and swinging a knife. The man also chased the mother while still holding the knife. When he was taken into custody, he called the family "terrorists" and vowed to kill them when released from jail. Acting U.S. Attorney Mary Jane Stewart said of the attack, "The cowardly and unprovoked attack and display of hate-filled aggression by this defendant toward two innocent young girls and their father is despicable. An attack upon the free exercise of any person's religious beliefs is an attack on that person's civil rights. The Department of Justice will continue to vigorously prosecute such violent acts motivated by hate.[[628]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-629)

In 2020, it was reported that Muslim detainees at a federal immigration facility in [Miami](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Miami "Miami"), Florida, were repeatedly served pork or pork-based products against their religious beliefs, according to claims made by immigrant advocates.[[629]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-:02-630)[[630]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-:12-631)[[631]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-:22-632) The Muslim detainees at the Krome detention facility in Miami were forced to eat pork because religiously compliant/[halal](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Halal "Halal") meals that ICE served had been consistently rotten and expired.[[629]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-:02-630) In one instance, the [Chaplain](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chaplain "Chaplain") at Krome allegedly dismissed pleas from Muslim detainees for help, saying, "It is what it is."[[630]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-:12-631) Civil rights groups said many had suffered illness, like stomach pains, vomiting, and diarrhea, as a result.[[630]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-:12-631) An ICE spokesman said, "Any claim that ICE denies reasonable and equitable opportunity for persons to observe their religious dietary practices is false."[[632]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-apne_Groups_Muslim-633) Previously in 2019, a Pakistani-born man with a valid US work permit was reportedly given nothing but pork sandwiches for six consecutive days.[[630]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-:12-631)

##### Wrongful detentions

[[edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Persecution_of_Muslims&action=edit&section=65 "Edit section: Wrongful detentions")]

In the aftermath of the [September 11 attacks](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/September_11_attacks "September 11 attacks"), Arabs and Muslims complained of increased scrutiny and racial profiling at airports. In a poll conducted by the _[Boston Globe](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Boston\_Globe "Boston Globe")_, 71 percent of Blacks and 57 percent of Whites believed that "Arabs and Arab-Americans should undergo special, more intensive security checks before boarding airplanes." Some Muslims and Arabs have complained of being held without explanation and subjected to hours of questioning and arrest without cause. Such cases have led to lawsuits being filed by the ACLU. Fox News radio host [Mike Gallagher](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mike_Gallagher_(political_commentator) "Mike Gallagher (political commentator)") suggested that airports have a "Muslims Only" line in the wake of the 9/11 attacks stating "It's time to have a Muslims check-point line in America's airports and have Muslims be scrutinized. You better believe it, it's time." In Queens, New York, Muslims and Arabs have complained that the NYPD is unfairly targeting Muslim communities in raids tied to the alleged Zazi terror plot.

##### Criticism of the war on terror

[[edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Persecution_of_Muslims&action=edit&section=66 "Edit section: Criticism of the war on terror")]

Main article: [Criticism of the war on terror](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Criticism_of_the_war_on_terror "Criticism of the war on terror")

See also: [War on Islam controversy](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/War_on_Islam_controversy "War on Islam controversy")

The war on terror has been labelled a war against Islam by ex-[United States Attorney General](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States_Attorney_General "United States Attorney General")[Ramsey Clark](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ramsey_Clark "Ramsey Clark"), who said that "Most of the politicians are putting it as Islamic terrorists but what they really mean is the threat of Islam. So the idea of the war on Islam is the idea of extermination of a proportion never seen in history at any time."[[633]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-634)

There is no widely agreed on figure for the number of people that have been killed so far in the War on Terror as it has been defined by the Bush Administration to include the [war in Afghanistan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/War_in_Afghanistan_(2001%E2%80%932021) "War in Afghanistan (2001–2021)"), the [war in Iraq](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iraq_War "Iraq War"), and operations elsewhere. The [International Physicians for the Prevention of Nuclear War](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Physicians_for_the_Prevention_of_Nuclear_War "International Physicians for the Prevention of Nuclear War"), and the Physicians for Social Responsibility and Physicians for Global Survival give total estimates ranging from 1.3 million to 2 million casualties.[[634]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-635) Another study from 2018 by Brown University's [Watson Institute for International and Public Affairs](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Watson_Institute_for_International_and_Public_Affairs "Watson Institute for International and Public Affairs") puts the total number of casualties of the War on Terror in Iraq, Afghanistan, and [Pakistan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pakistan "Pakistan") between 480,000 and 507,000.[[635]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-636) A 2019 Brown University study places the number of direct deaths caused by the War on Terror at over 800,000 when [Syria](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Syria "Syria") and [Yemen](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yemen "Yemen") are included, with the toll rising to 3.1 million or more once indirect deaths are taken into account.[[636]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-637)

### Oceania

[[edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Persecution_of_Muslims&action=edit&section=67 "Edit section: Oceania")]

#### New Zealand

[[edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Persecution_of_Muslims&action=edit&section=68 "Edit section: New Zealand")]

The [Christchurch mosque shootings](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christchurch_mosque_shootings "Christchurch mosque shootings") were two consecutive [white supremacist](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/White_supremacy "White supremacy")[terrorist attacks](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Terrorist_attacks "Terrorist attacks") which were committed at the [Al Noor Mosque](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Al_Noor_Mosque,_Christchurch "Al Noor Mosque, Christchurch") and the [Linwood Islamic Centre](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linwood_Islamic_Centre "Linwood Islamic Centre") in [Christchurch](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christchurch "Christchurch"), [New Zealand](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand "New Zealand"), during [Friday prayers](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Friday_prayer "Friday prayer") on 15 March 2019.[[637]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-638)[[638]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-:9-639)[[639]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-:10-640)[[640]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-stuff-111313938-641)[[641]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-abc-109044162-642)[[642]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-Stuff_1113430932-643)[_[excessive citations](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing\_sources#Bundling\_citations "Wikipedia:Citing sources")_] The attacks killed 51 people[[643]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-RNZ50Dead-644)[[644]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-ABC50Dead-645) and injured 40 others.[[645]](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_note-rnz00-646)

By other Muslim groups
----------------------

[[edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Persecution_of_Muslims&action=edit&section=69 "Edit section: By other Muslim groups")]

See also: [Sectarian violence among Muslims](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sectarian_violence_among_Muslims "Sectarian violence among Muslims"), [Salafi–Sufi relations](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Salafi%E2%80%93Sufi_relations "Salafi–Sufi relations"), and [Shia–Sunni relations](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shia%E2%80%93Sunni_relations "Shia–Sunni relations")

Persecution of Muslims by other Muslims includes [Persecution of minority Muslim groups](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_minority_Muslim_groups "Persecution of minority Muslim groups"), [Anti-Shi'ism](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anti-Shi%27ism "Anti-Shi'ism"), [Anti-Sunnism](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anti-Sunnism "Anti-Sunnism"), [Persecution of Ahmadis](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Ahmadis "Persecution of Ahmadis"), [Persecution of Hazara people](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Hazara_people "Persecution of Hazara people"), [Persecution of Kashmiri Shias](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Kashmiri_Shias "Persecution of Kashmiri Shias"), and [Persecution of Sufis](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Sufis "Persecution of Sufis").

[ISBN](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISBN_(identifier) "ISBN (identifier)")[978-0300100983](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0300100983 "Special:BookSources/978-0300100983"). 374.
127.   **[^](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_ref-127 "Jump up")**["Algeria - Colonialism, Resistance, Revolution | Britannica"](https://www.britannica.com/place/Algeria/Colonial-rule). _www.britannica.com_. 9 September 2025. Retrieved 11 September 2025. It is difficult to gauge in human terms the losses suffered by Algerians during the early years of the French occupation. Estimates of the number of those dead from disease and starvation and as a direct result of warfare during the early years of colonization vary considerably, but the most reliable ones indicate that the native population of Algeria fell by nearly one-third in the years between the French invasion and the end of fighting in the mid-1870s.
128.   **[^](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_ref-128 "Jump up")**Jalata, Asafa (2016). [_Phases of Terrorism in the Age of Globalization: From Christopher Columbus to Osama bin Laden_](https://books.google.com/books?id=SCjxCgAAQBAJ&pg=PA92). Palgrave Macmillan US. pp.92–3. [ISBN](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISBN_(identifier) "ISBN (identifier)")[978-1-137-55234-1](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1-137-55234-1 "Special:BookSources/978-1-137-55234-1"). [Archived](https://web.archive.org/web/20240328160439/https://books.google.com/books?id=SCjxCgAAQBAJ&pg=PA92#v=onepage&q&f=false) from the original on 28 March 2024. Retrieved 17 May 2020. Within the first three decades, the French military massacred between half a million to one million from approximately three million Algerian people.
129.   **[^](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_ref-Kiernan2007_129-0 "Jump up")**[Kiernan, Ben](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ben_Kiernan "Ben Kiernan") (2007). [_Blood and Soil: A World History of Genocide and Extermination from Sparta to Darfur_](https://archive.org/details/bloodan_kie_2007_00_0326). Yale University Press. pp.[364](https://archive.org/details/bloodan_kie_2007_00_0326/page/364)–ff. [ISBN](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISBN_(identifier) "ISBN (identifier)")[978-0-300-10098-3](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-0-300-10098-3 "Special:BookSources/978-0-300-10098-3"). In Algeria, colonization and genocidal massacres proceeded in tandem. From 1830 to 1847, its European settler population quadrupled to 104,000. Of the native Algerian population of approximately 3 million in 1830, about 500,000 to 1 million perished in the first three decades of French conquest.

433.   **[^](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persecution_of_Muslims#cite_ref-433 "Jump up")**[Swaminathan S. Anklesaria Aiyar](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swaminathan_S._Anklesaria_Aiyar "Swaminathan S. Anklesaria Aiyar") (24 November 2020). ["Despite Modi, India Has Not Yet Become a Hindu Authoritarian State"](https://www.cato.org/policy-analysis/despite-modi-india-has-not-yet-become-hindu-authoritarian-state). [CATO Institute](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/CATO_Institute "CATO Institute"). But fears of India becoming a Hindu authoritarian state have been voiced after Narendra Modi of the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) came to power in New Delhi in 2014. The party's Hindutva philosophy—the creation of a great Hindu state—envisages a Hindu state where citizens with other religious beliefs are tolerated but have second-class status. The BJP has been associated with hundreds of violent Hindu-Muslim riots over the decades, the latest beingin Delhi in February 2020, which claimed 54 lives.
